< text>
Magic Kingdom is a perfect room for newer players. We plan on bringing our 10 and 6 year olds back to do this room. The path is clear for what you want to do, but the puzzles aren't so easy that you quickly figure out how to accomplish each goal. Having that kind of clarity helped  newer players enjoy and not get too frustrated. It is technologically and visually very well done, and probably my favorite of the dozen or so rooms I have done. Everyone should experience this room.<//text>

< time>
1543281293193<//time>
<Rating>2<//Rating>< Review>
From a Vendor point of view: Wednesday's space fee is way overpriced @ $25. Hardly any customers show up. Vendors are allowed to sell fake name brands such as Michael Kors, Adidas, Nike Pink as well as others and none of the staff says anything. This makes it really hard on the vendors who go out and by the real items and try to complete reselling against the fakes. Not Right and its illegal. The management of the Madera flea market should consider advertising more or doing something to draw more customers in and make it a better experience for all. It's time to stop raking in the money and telling all the vendors what they can't do and maybe try telling the vendors what you have done for them since they're the only reason that the entire flea market is open. Everybody steps on the little guy until he becomes your boss. On a positive note the food is great the vegetables look fabulous and most of the vendors are pretty nice, even most of the staff seem to have a real positive attitude.

I tell one, I tell all, come support the vendors at all the flea markets. Come and have a great time. Come and eat some delicious food. Take home some very unique and fabulous items. But remember the vendors work hard to pick, front the cash and buy this stuff for you. They can't sell it at a cheaper price than they paid, so please be considerate in your negotiations and don't insult a vendor buy offering half the price,  that they are asking. If you can't come somewhat close to their asking price  just being nice say thank you and move on. You have so many choices  that you don't have to insult the vendor, just a little word of advice.< /Review>

<Rating>3< /Rating><review>One busy place on Sunday. The Wed event is smaller, Sunday is huge. Mostly low quality clothing and such, but lots of good produce and hard to find seasonings and cooking stuff. The cheap new clothing is overpriced and isn't worth your hard earned money. Even had a Santa booth for the kiddos to take pics with him, and mini horse rides and even masseuse services. Lotta good food. Costs two bucks each person to get in. Very little of what is usually thought of for a swap meet, people selling their old stuff like tools or lawn furniture or whatever, it's almost all vendors with new stuff.
